/*

CALCULATE; 
CREATE MEMBER CURRENTCUBE.[Measures].[Sales Average]
 AS [Measures].[Sales] / [Measures].[Fact Days Count], 
VISIBLE = 1 ,  ASSOCIATED_MEASURE_GROUP = 'Fact Shipments'  ;           
CREATE MEMBER CURRENTCUBE.[Measures].[Gross Profit]
 AS [Measures].[Sales]-[Measures].[Accounting Cost], 
FORMAT_STRING = "$#,##0.00;($#,##0.00)", 
VISIBLE = 1 ,  ASSOCIATED_MEASURE_GROUP = 'Fact Shipments';      
CREATE MEMBER CURRENTCUBE.[Measures].[Orders]
 AS [Measures].[Order Num2 Distinct Count], 
FORMAT_STRING = "#,##0;-#,##0", 
VISIBLE = 1 ,  ASSOCIATED_MEASURE_GROUP = 'Fact Shipments';          
CREATE MEMBER CURRENTCUBE.[Measures].[FP % Sales]
 AS ([Measures].[Freight Charged]-[Measures].[Freight Cost])/[Measures].[Sales], 
FORMAT_STRING = "Percent", 
VISIBLE = 1 ,  ASSOCIATED_MEASURE_GROUP = 'Fact Shipments';         
CREATE MEMBER CURRENTCUBE.[Measures].[FP % GP]
 AS ([Measures].[Freight Charged]-[Measures].[Freight Cost])/([Measures].[Sales]-[Measures].[Accounting Cost]), 
FORMAT_STRING = "Percent", 
VISIBLE = 1 ,  ASSOCIATED_MEASURE_GROUP = 'Fact Shipments';         
CREATE MEMBER CURRENTCUBE.[Measures].[GP% After Freight]
 AS (([Measures].[Sales]-[Measures].[Accounting Cost])+([Measures].[Freight Charged]-[Measures].[Freight Cost]))/[Measures].[Sales], 
FORMAT_STRING = "Percent", 
VISIBLE = 1 ,  ASSOCIATED_MEASURE_GROUP = 'Fact Shipments';  
CREATE MEMBER CURRENTCUBE.[Measures].[FP % Freight/Sales]
 AS [Measures].[Freight Charged]/[Measures].[Sales], 
FORMAT_STRING = "Percent", 
VISIBLE = 1 ,  ASSOCIATED_MEASURE_GROUP = 'Fact Shipments';         
CREATE MEMBER CURRENTCUBE.[Measures].[GP%]
 AS ([Measures].[Sales]-[Measures].[Accounting Cost])/[Measures].[Sales], 
FORMAT_STRING = "Percent", 
VISIBLE = 1 ,  ASSOCIATED_MEASURE_GROUP = 'Fact Shipments';          
CREATE MEMBER CURRENTCUBE.[Measures].[Freight Profit]
 AS [Measures].[Freight Charged]-[Measures].[Freight Cost], 
FORMAT_STRING = "$#,##0.00;($#,##0.00)", 
VISIBLE = 1 ,  ASSOCIATED_MEASURE_GROUP = 'Fact Shipments'; </Text>
